## Maps

### Description
Each map will have Wins, Losses, K/D, and Top agents. I should be able to also query top X maps

Now the interesting thing about Top agents is they are icons with their own win percentage written below them. So what I want from this is just the name (which we can get from the ALT of the icon), and corresponding win rate. These top agents can be 1, 2, 3 (based on what I see) 

And when we're returning the response, we can include the agent details from the agentData.js along with the winrate attached for the map

As for the map, attach relevant Map Details from https://valorant-api.com/v1/maps. Name, splash image URL, displayIcon would be nice. You can save this on startup as well like we did for agents

### Example URL
Unrated: https://tracker.gg/valorant/profile/riot/Spider31415%236921/maps?platform=pc&playlist=unrated
Competitive: https://tracker.gg/valorant/profile/riot/Spider31415%236921/maps?platform=pc&playlist=competitive
